It may be related to the large crowds during the festival, but the quality of the dishes in the hotel's Chinese restaurant truly embodies Jinling. The level is far higher than the level of high-scoring restaurants that buy points on various platforms. If you want to eat well-made Huaiyang cuisine, you don‚Äôt need to queue up at those Internet celebrity restaurants. In particular, there are several hidden dishes that are not on the menu recommended by the glasses girl at Chaohu Hall. See pictures 1-4 below.
